I stop by every time im in walnut creek. I love the rolled icecream. When it melts it has a pleasant texture, not filmy like regular icecream. Its a fun experience to watch as well. My all time favorite is the ferrero rocher but the red velvet is yummy too. <text>Tiny place with amazing food! My girlfriend and I decided to try this place on a friend's recommendation. When we first showed up, I wasn't impressed. It's a hole in the wall between a mexican food shop and a liquor store. The people inside were hustling. taking orders over the phone, working the grill, prepping food. They were very nice, but busy! The menu is small, but that's not a bad thing. We ordered a pulled pork sandwich and a twist burger. The food took a bit of time to make (maybe 15 minutes) but the results were amazing. The food was just awesome. the pulled pork sandwich was good sized and mouth watering. the Twist burger (I only had one bite because my GF didn't want to share) was juicy and topped with the perfect blend and amount of toppings. <user_id>110439657338712385664<//user_id><username>Andy Stinson</username><time>1464500450405<//time>< rating>
5</rating>
< text>
I'm on a perennial quest for San Diego's best burger.  Crazee Burgers to Habit and Smash, I've tried them all.  Trump card in the local Burger Wars is Twitz, a hole-in-the-wall on a no-man's part of University Avenue sandwiched between Hillcrest and North Park.  It took me half-an-hour, and a "give-me-directions" to find this joint.  It was well worth the effort.  I arrived a little frustrated.  Dylan, the Maitre d', cashier and general manager quickly erased my frustration; he has passion for his crafted burgers and an accommodating friendliness that's  refreshing.  My opinion is that this is the best burger in San Diego.  If you've gotta better salvo in the burger wars, then I'd love to hear your recommendation.

Andy Stinson< /text>

<review>Call before you go.

I went before they opened. They opened almost on time. That day, they had a catering order. So as soon as I walk in, I am advised that I can only order rolls. No bentos, soups, meat, or the like. So I ended up ordering 3 rolls for just shy of $40. A pricey lunch for me.

Rice was moist. I was happy with the portion of avocado slices on my Caterpiller roll. The Washington roll had clean salmon. The last roll was a simple California roll, so pretty hard to mess that up.

Service was mostly attentive (ordering to go). But the inability to plan ahead knowing you have a large catering order and not being able to stock enough food before you even open says a lot to me. Additionally, it took about 35 to 40 minutes to get my order. With a 30 minute lunch time, I cant afford to come here again.

Overall I give it 3 stars for food quality hindered by slow prep time and inability to purchase enough food supplies for the daily lunch crowd. I doubt I would return unless I was really hurting for a nearby Japanese food fix.<//review>< pictures>
None</pictures>

<UserId.>116319166869555900344< /UserId.><Name>F Lew< /Name><date>1592609308313</date><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
Dr Dao is AWESOME!!! I tried to set up telehealth new patient appt with Dr Dao, but mom didn't know how to set up & use the link, so Dr Dao called my mom for a phone consult free of charge because she just wanted to help my mom. (Of course I called her office later to make sure the appt was processed bc I definitely didn't want to take advantage of her goodwill.)

Dr Dao genuinely cares for the wellbeing of her patients.  Our 1st conference call was cut short bc Dr Dao had a surgery patient waiting, but despite being fully booked, Dr found time to call my mom back a 2nd time to make sure all my mom's questions were answered to her satisfaction.

Dr Dao has a very warm, caring and calming voice, super knowledgeable about all ENT issues, saw a couple photos and immediately diagnosed the problem. (My mom had multiple issues!) Dr Dao was BEYOND patient with my mom, listening to all her questions, never rushing, never interrupting.  Dr Dao is exceptionally skilled at handling & interacting with elderly/senior patients.  My mom is definitely in the "difficult patient" category (generally combative and disagreeable), but in the end Dr Dao even won over my mom!

My mom is super paranoid about new medications, so Dr Dao ran down a list of various treatment options (both over the counter & Rx drugs), explaining how each type of med worked.  Brilliant strategy bc my mom felt she was in control of her meds since she could choose which meds to use.

I'm so glad Dr Dao accepts telehealth patients, and so grateful she was available.  She is everything you would hope for and expect in a physician and more.  I would highly recommend her, and plan to use her for my family if I ever need an ENT.</Text>
